style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;-- Intel Corporation today reported </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">-quarter revenue of </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">$13.8 billion</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, operating income of </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">$3.8 billion</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, net income of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$2.8 billion</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;and EPS of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$0.55</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. The company generated approximately </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$5.5 billion</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in cash from operations, paid dividends of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$1.1 billion</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, and used </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$2.1 billion</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;to repurchase </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">74 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;shares of stock.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8220;Our second-quarter results showed the strength of our strategy to extend the reach of Intel technology from the data center to PCs to the Internet of Things,&#8221; said Intel CEO Brian Krzanich. &#8220;With the ramp of our Baytrail SoC family, we have expanded into new segments such as Chrome-based systems, and we are on track to meet our 40 million unit tablet goal. In addition, we&#160;hit an important qualification milestone for our upcoming 14nm Broadwell product, and expect the first systems to be on shelves during the holidays.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Intel announced that it intends to return more cash to shareholders by lowering its cash balance further through increased share repurchases. The board of directors authorized an increase of $20 billion to its share repurchase program and the company is forecasting share repurchases of approximately $4 billion in the third quarter, with additional share repurchases in the fourth quarter. Over the last decade Intel has returned almost $90 billion to shareholders through dividends and share repurchases.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">"This change in our capital structure is the continuation of a multi-year focus on creating value and returning cash to our shareholders, and reinforces our confidence in the business," said Stacy J. Smith, Intel CFO and executive vice president. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><br><div It was a good quarter representing financial growth and solid momentum as we approach the second half of the year.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Second-quarter revenue of </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">$13.8B</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">up 8%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;sequentially, above the average seasonal increase in the second quarter and in line with our revised outlook on June 12. Gross margin of </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">64.5%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">up</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;almost 5 points from the first quarter and 1.5 points above our original Q2 guidance. The almost five point increase relative to the first quarter is primarily due to lower 14nm startup costs, higher platform* volumes, and lower platform* unit costs. Net income for the second quarter was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$2.8B</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;with earnings per share of </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">$0.55</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">In the second quarter we repurchased $2.1B of stock. We have also announced an additional $20 billion of authorizations for future stock repurchases. Our intent is to repurchase another $4B of stock in Q3 with additional repurchases planned for Q4. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Looking forward, we are forecasting revenue of </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">$14.4B</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the third quarter, up approximately 4 percent from the second quarter, this forecast is in line with the average seasonal increase for Q3 that we have seen over the last several years. We expect third-quarter gross margin to increase by </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">1.5</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;points to </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">66%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, driven by lower platform* unit costs and higher platform* volumes, partially offset by lower platform* average selling prices.
